## Mircroelectronics & VLSI Design

- Compound Semiconductor based emitter and detector
- Low Power High Performance circuit designs
- Soft error tolerant circuits
- VLSI Testing and Hardware Security
- Reliability Modeling of Semiconductor Devices

## Power System

- Robust and Efficient System Operation and Planning
- Renewable integration in power system
- Operation and Control of Microgrid

## Communication Systems

- Smart Metering, Powerline Communication and IoT
- Cognitive Radio, Physical Layer Security, and FSO
- NOMA, Molecular Communication, and THz Communication
- UAV Based Communication and 5G Architecture
- Wireless Powered Communication

## RF and Microwave

- Microwave and Millimeter Wave Polarization Converters
- Microwave Absorbers and Cloaking
- Microwave and Millimeter Wave Antennas for 5G, Metamaterials
- Microsatellite Antenna Design and Computational EM
- Drone Detection and Anti Drone Systems

## Signal and Image Processing

- Underwater Signal Processing
- Image and Video Processing
- Speech and Audio Signal Processing
- Machine Learning
- Medical Instrumentation

## Power Electronics

- Converters for Renewable Energy and Electric Vehicles
- WBG based High gain DC-DC Converters
- Design and Development of on board Chargers
- Smart Electric Transportation
- Grid Ties Solar Inverters

Dr. Arun Kumar Verma
Senior Member IEEE, USA
Member, IEEE IES Technical Committee on Power Electronics 2024. USA
Member, IEEE IES Technical Committee on Smart Grid, 2025. USA
Associate Professor, Department of Electrical Engineering
Indian Institute of Technology Jammu, India
E-mail: arun.verma@iitjammu.ac.in, arunverma59@gmail.com
Contact: +91-9549650188, 0191-2741225
Associate Editor for IEEE Transactions on Transportation Electrification.
Associate Editor for IEEE Emerging and Selected Topics in Industrial Electronics
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
Brief
Dr. Arun Kumar Verma earned his master’s and Ph.D. from I.I.T. Delhi, New Delhi, India. He served as a visiting professor at Ontario Tech
University, Oshawa, Ontario, Canada, in 2024. He was a post-doctoral research fellow (PDF) at the Energy Research Institute (ERI@N),
Nanyang Technological University (NTU) Singapore, from 2015 to 2016. Before joining NTU Singapore, he worked as a visiting graduate
researcher (VGR) at the Smart Grid Energy Research Center (SMERC), University of California Los Angeles (UCLA), California, USA, from
2014-2015. He won the prestigious BASE fellowship for advanced solar energy research in 2014. He has been conferred with the prestigious
POSOCO Power System Research Award 2016. He also won the SERB SIRE fellowship. He is an associate editor for IEEE Transactions on
Transportation Electrification and also Associate editor for IEEE Emerging and Selected Topics in Indistrial Electronics.. He is a guest editor in
the IET Power Electronics special issue, an assistant editor of the smart grid journal, and a member of the editorial board for EPE Journal. His
research interests include power electronics, converters for renewable energy and EV chargers, bi-directional power flow, and electric
transportation.

#### Priyanka Mishra

Priyanka Mishra completed her Bachelor’s in Electrical Engineering from Galgotia’s College of Engineering and Technology, India in 2013. She received her M. Tech and Ph. D. degrees in Energy Science and Engineering from Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur, India in 2017 and 2022, respectively. Her Masters’ work won as best post award by Indian Institute of Technology Kharagpur, India. Her Ph. D. work is awarded by POSOCO, India in doctoral category as one of the best Ph. D. Thesis in Power Systems. She worked as a Postdoctoral Associate at State University of New York at Stony Brook, New York, USA from April, 2022 to October, 2023. Key milestones during this research were development of provably resilient, programmable networked microgrids. She worked as HVDC Control and Protection Engineer at GE Renewables, Noida, India from November 2023 to January 2026. Out of her research, she published 7 journals and 5 conference papers, including one book chapter. She received outstanding reviewer award in IEEE Journal of Ocean Engineering in 2022. Her research interests include solar photovoltaic power generation and power system protection integrating inverter-based renewable energy sources.

##### Research Interest

Protection of microgrid integrating renewable energy sources (solar power, wind power, etc); Neural active fault management control of power-electronic converter-based renewable energy sources; Time-domain relaying; Converter transformer protection.

##### Education Qualification

1. Ph.D. in ENERGY SCIENCE AND ENGINEERING from INDIAN INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY KHARAGPUR (2017-2022)
2. M.Tech. in ENERGY SCIENCE AND ENGINEERING from INDIAN INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY KHARAGPUR (2015-2017)
3. B.Tech. in ELECTRICAL ENGINEERING from GALGOTIAS COLLEGE OF ENGINEERING AND TECHNOLOGY (2009-2013)
4. 12th in MATHEMATICS, PHYSICS, CHEMISTRY from NAVYUG KANYA INTER COLLEGE, RAJENDRA NAGAR, LUCKNOW (2007-2008)
5. 10th from NAVYUG KANYA INTER COLLEGE, RAJENDRA NAGAR, LUCKNOW (2005-2006)

##### Academic Interests

Power Systems; Switchgear and protection devices; Power System Operation and Control

##### Research Experience

Postdoctoral Associate at Stony Brook University, NY, USA from April 2022 to October 2023.

System Engineer - Control and Protection at GE Renewable Energy, India from November 2023 to January 2026.

##### Publications

#### Priyatosh Jena

I am Dr. Priyatosh Jena, currently serving as an Assistant Professor in the Department of Electrical Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Jammu. I received my Ph.D. degree in Electrical Engineering from the Indian Institute of Technology (Banaras Hindu University), Varanasi, India, my M.Tech. degree in Electrical Engineering with specialization in Renewable Energy and Energy Management from the National Institute of Technology Arunachal Pradesh, India, and my B.Tech. degree in Electrical and Electronics Engineering from the International Institute of Information Technology, Bhubaneswar, India. I am a member of the IEEE Power Electronics Society (PELS) Educational Videos Committee. I was awarded the Chairman’s Gold Medal and the Institute Gold Medal from NIT Arunachal Pradesh in recognition of outstanding academic performance in the M.Tech program. I am also a recipient of the 14th GRID-INDIA Power System Awards (GIPSA) 2025–26.

##### Research Interest

Battery Charging System, Bidirectional Converter, Reconfigurable Power Converter, and Soft-Switched Converter.

##### Education Qualification

1. **Ph.D. in Electrical Engineering (2019–2025)**

Indian Institute of Technology (Banaras Hindu University), Varanasi, India

**Thesis Title:** *Soft-Switching Modulation Techniques for Bidirectional Dual Active Bridge Converter Based Battery Charging Systems*

**Supervisor:** Prof. Rajeev Kumar Singh and Prof. Vivek Nandan Lal
2. **M.Tech. in Renewable Energy and Energy Management (2016–2018)**

National Institute of Technology Arunachal Pradesh, India

**Thesis Title:** *Simulation and Study of Solar Powered Water Pumping System using BLDC Motor*

**Supervisor:** Dr. Rajen Pudur
3. **B.Tech. in Electrical and Electronics Engineering (2011–2015)**

International Institute of Information Technology Bhubaneswar, India

##### Academic Interests

Digital Control of Power Converters, Electric Vehicle Technology and Charging Systems, Network Theory, Power Converter Design, Power Quality and FACTS Devices, Renewable Energy Systems, and Switch Mode Power Supplies.

##### Teaching Engagements

1. Power Engineering (Even Semester 2026).

2. Power Engineering Lab (Even Semester 2026).

3. Physical Electronics (Odd Semister 2026).

##### Research Experience

Bidirectional Converters, Electric Vehicle Charging Systems, Dual Active Bridge Converters Maximum Power Point Tracking, Renewable Energy Systems, Soft-Switched Converters

##### Publications

##### Administrative Responsibilities

1. Professor In-Charge/Returing Officer for the Election Commission for 2026-27 at IIT Jammu.

##### Awards & honours

**A1. GRID-INDIA Power System Award (GIPSA) – Ph.D. Category (2025–26)**

Awarded to **Priyatosh Jena** for outstanding doctoral research titled *“Soft-Switching Modulation Techniques for Bidirectional Dual Active Bridge Converter Based Battery Charging Systems.”* The award is conferred under the CSR initiative of Grid Controller of India Limited (GRID-INDIA), formerly Power System Operation Corporation Limited (POSOCO), recognizing exemplary Ph.D. research contributions in power systems and allied domains.

**A2. Best Thesis Award – IEEE STPEC 2025, Goa**

**Priyatosh Jena** received the **Best Ph.D. Thesis Award** at the 2025 4th IEEE International Conference on Smart Technologies for Power, Energy and Control (STPEC) 2025 held in Goa, India, for the doctoral thesis titled *“Soft-Switching Modulation Techniques for Bidirectional Dual Active Bridge Converter Based Battery Charging Systems.”*

**A3. Chairman’s Gold Medal (2018)**

Awarded to **Priyatosh Jena** for securing the **highest CGPA among all students of the Electrical Engineering branch** in the postgraduate program (2016–2018) at National Institute of Technology Arunachal Pradesh. The medal was presented during the **5th Convocation** by the Chief Guest Sanjay Hemant Inamdar.

**A4. Institute Gold Medal (2018)**

Awarded to **Priyatosh Jena** for achieving the **highest CGPA in the Renewable Energy and Energy Management M.Tech. program** offered by the Department of Electrical Engineering at National Institute of Technology Arunachal Pradesh. The medal was presented during the **5th Convocation** by Anil Dattatraya Sahasrabudhe, Chairman of All India Council for Technical Education (AICTE).

I have openings for PhD students in the area of Power Electronics and Energy Conversion Systems, including AC-DC/DC-DC converters and related topics. Candidates with a good background in power electronics, control systems, and circuit design are encouraged to apply. Interested students may contact me for more details.

#### Soma S Dhavala

Soma S. Dhavala is an AI researcher, technologist, and educator with over two decades of experience spanning machine learning, statistics, signal processing, distributed systems, and large-scale AI platforms. He has held leadership roles across academia, industry, startups, and social-impact AI initiatives, including at Wadhwani AI, where he led initiatives in agriculture, public health, education, and Generative AI. His work combines deep theoretical grounding in Bayesian statistics, applied mathematics, and machine learning with hands-on expertise in building scalable AI systems and products. Off late, his focus has increasingly shifted toward Frontier Model Development, including LLMs, multimodal AI systems, interoperability frameworks, and reliable AI architectures for real-world deployment, focusing on sovereign and resource efficiency

##### Research Interest

1. Frontier Models and Large Language Models (LLMs)
2. Generative AI and Multimodal AI
3. Reliable and Trustworthy AI
4. AI Systems and ML Infrastructure
5. Bayesian Statistics and Probabilistic Modeling
6. Uncertainty Quantification in Machine Learning
7. Approximate Bayesian Inference and MCMC
8. Deep Learning and Representation Learning
9. AI for Agriculture, Healthcare, and Education
10. Learning Analytics and AI for EdTech
11. Statistical Signal Processing
12. Dynamical Systems and Computational Mathematics
13. Distributed and Scalable Machine Learning
14. Explainable and Interoperable AI
15. Quantization and Efficient ML Systems
16. Edge AI and IoT-enabled Intelligent Systems
17. Scientific Computing and High-Performance Computing
18. Applied AI for Social Impact
19. AI & Robotics
20. Hardware Accelerators for AI

##### Education Qualification

1. Ph.D (Statistics), Texas A & M University, 2010
2. M.S (Applied Maths), University of Washington, 2022
3. M.S (EE), IIT Madras, 2000
4. B.E (ECE), S.R.K.R. Engg. College, 1997

##### Academic Interests

1. Developing a unified theoretical understanding of Deep Learning and Frontier Models, including questions around representation learning, generalization, scaling laws, optimization dynamics, and reasoning capabilities in large-scale neural systems.
2. Understanding why Deep Learning works from first principles by bridging ideas across statistics, optimization, information theory, dynamical systems, signal processing, and computational neuroscience.
3. Building reliable, trustworthy, and uncertainty-aware AI systems, especially for Large Language Models (LLMs), multimodal systems, and real-world deployment scenarios.
4. Designing scalable AI systems and ML infrastructure for distributed training and inference of GPT-scale and Frontier Models, including efficient architectures, quantization, interoperability, and systems optimization.
5. Developing curriculum and training frameworks for systems programmers and AI engineers that integrate distributed systems, high-performance computing, ML systems engineering, and large-scale model development.
6. Bayesian statistics, probabilistic modeling, approximate inference, and uncertainty quantification in high-dimensional machine learning systems.
7. Generative AI, multimodal learning, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), and document intelligence systems.
8. AI for Education, Agriculture, Healthcare, and public-interest technology, with emphasis on deployable, scalable, and inclusive AI ecosystems.
9. Explainable AI, interoperable ML systems, and democratization of AI through open architectures, tooling, and platform-centric approaches.
10. Scientific computing, computational mathematics, signal processing, dynamical systems, and their intersections with modern AI.

##### Research Experience

IPR, Monitoring & Evaluation for AI Programs — Indian Institute of Technology Jammu / Central Project Management Unit (CPMU), Ministry of Education (2024–2025) :

Contributed to initiatives around Intellectual Property Rights (IPR), Monitoring, Evaluation, and Learning (MEL) frameworks for AI-focused national programs and innovation ecosystems.

Applied Research in Machine Learning and Generative AI (LLMs) — Wadhwani AI (2020–2024): Led applied research initiatives in Machine Learning and Generative AI with a focus on Large Language Models (LLMs), Document Intelligence, AI for Agriculture, Public Health, and Education. Worked on scalable AI systems, retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), synthetic data generation, uncertainty-aware inference, and production-grade AI deployment for real-world impact.

EdTech, AI for Learning Systems, and AI Platforms (Public & Private Sector) — Various organizations including Embibe, EkStep Foundation, NIIT, and independent consulting engagements (2014–2019): Worked on AI-driven learning systems, recommendation engines, learning analytics, NLP-based educational tools, conversational analytics, ML platforms, and scalable architectures for digital education ecosystems serving both public and private sector initiatives.

Bayesian Statistics, Computational Biology, and High-Dimensional Inference — Texas A&M University (2005–2011): Ph.D. and Postdoctoral research focused on Bayesian semiparametric modeling, heterogeneous gene expression analysis, MCMC methods, high-dimensional graphical models, and uncertainty quantification.

Applied & Computational Mathematics, Signal Processing, and Distributed Estimation — University of Washington, Indian Institute of Technology Madras, and Iowa State University (1997–2005): Research work spanning dynamical systems, stochastic processes, deep learning foundations, time-frequency analysis, adaptive signal processing, and distributed estimation in wireless sensor networks.

##### Publications

​Lattice-Based Vector Quantization for Low-Bit Quantization-Aware Training Rishika Kohli, Soma S Dhavala, Shaifu Gupta, Manoj S. Gaur, Proceedings of the Machine Learning Research, Conference on Parsimony and Learning, 2026. ​​

QuantProb: Generalizing Probabilities along with Predictions for a Pre-trained Classifier , Aditya Challa, Soma S. Dhavla, Snehanshu Saha, 40th Conference on Uncertainty in Artificial Intelligence (UAI 2024), 2024.

Automatic Interpretation of Line Probe Assay Test for TB , Agrawal, J., Kumar, M., Tiwari, A., Danisetty, S., Dhavala, S., Jain, N., Balraj, P., Singh, N., Shingi, S., Kurada, J., Rao, R., Anand, S., & Kumar, N. (2024)., AAAI, 2024.

# HoD Message

- [Home](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)
- HoD Message

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/Ravikant Saini.jpg)

### Dr. Ravikant Saini

Head of Department

- [hod.ee@iitjammu.ac.in](mailto:hod.ee@iitjammu.ac.in)

## Dr. Ravikant Saini

#### Message

Welcome to the Department of Electrical Engineering, Indian
Institute of Technology Jammu. In line with the Institute's focus on academics-oriented
research, the department considers both teaching and research integral. The department
accommodates highly experienced and dedicated faculty members who are great teachers and
researchers in their respective domains. We are also supported by invaluable staff
members who discharge their duties efficiently and enthusiastically on the technical and
administrative front. We look for zealous young minds for our UG, PG, and PhD programs,
as they are our greatest strength.

Our department and the Institute's
instrumental/computational facility are well-equipped to execute research on various
fields of Electrical Engineering. Contemporarily and fundamentally, the overall growth
of our department and, consequently, of the Institute and society at large drives us.
Each member at all levels actively and innovatively contributes to reaching the utmost
development of our department. We welcome you to be a part of our department and our
endeavours.

# Vision and Mission

- [Home](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)
- Vision and Mission

### Vision and Mission

- [Home](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

### Vision of the Department

- To ensure excellence across a wide range of disciplines, professions, and arts
while encouraging investigation across disciplinary boundaries with creative
learning.
- To nurture holistic engineers to address global challenges through research,
innovation, inspiration, and influence.
- To educate the next generation of engineering leaders, create new knowledge,
serve society, and transform our society for the better.
- To provide students with a foundational understanding of a broad range of
disciplines followed by opportunities for in-depth study with hands-on in their
chosen fields.
- To advance impactful knowledge and practice.
- To attract talented professionals and academicians of the world: to create,
innovate, and discover the unknown.

### Mission of the Department

- To educate the next generation of engineering leaders, to create new knowledge,
and to serve the society and to transform our society for the better.
- To provide students with a foundational understanding of a broad range of
disciplines followed by the opportunity for in-depth study with hands-on
experience in a chosen discipline.
- Discovering and advancing knowledge and practice.
- To attract the most talented people in the world: to create, to innovate, and to
see the unseen

#### Ankit Dubey

##### Education Qualification

Ankit received the B.E. degree in Electronics and Telecommunication Engineering from the Chhattisgarh Swami Vivekanand Technical University (CSVTU), Bhilai, India in 2009 and the Ph.D. degree in Electrical Engineering from the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT), Delhi, India in 2014. In 2012 and 2013, he was a visiting research scholar at the University of British Columbia, Vancouver, Canada.

##### Academic Interests

**Teaching Interests:**

- **UG**

- Communications Engineering
- Digital Design and Microcomputers
- Signals and Systems
- Control Theory
- Digital Communications
- Control Theory
- **PG**

- Digital Communications
- Detection and Estimation Theory
- Signal Theory
- Wireless Communication
- Information Theory and Coding
- Introduction to IoT

**Research Interests:**

- **Communications Theory:**

- Diversity Combining
- Multihop Transmission
- Physical Layer Security
- Machine-to-Machine Communication
- **Application Based**:

- Smart Solutions and IoT
- Use of SDR for Defence Applications

**B.Tech. Projects:**

- Smart Energy Metering-I: Mr. Kuldeep (2016UCS) and Mr. Ayush (2016UEE)
- Transmitter Localization: Ms. Dhriti (2017UEE)
- Smart Fire Emergency Response System: Mr. Kshitij (2017UEE)
- Smart Energy Metering-II: Mr. Abhyam (2018UCS), Mr. Abhishek (2018UCS), Mr. Deepansh (2018UCS)

**M.Tech. Projects:**

- Software Defined FMCW Radar for Detection & Ranging: Mr. Palash (2019PEE)
- Innovative Jammer for Pysical Layer Security: Ms. Navjot (2020PEE)

##### Research Experience

**Research Positions:**

- Jan 2019 - Present: Assistant Professor at Indian Institute of Technology Jammu, Jammu, J&K, India
- Dec 2014 - Jan 2019: Assistant Professor at National Institute of Technology Goa, Farmagudi, Ponda, Goa, India
- Jul 2014 - Dec 2014: Research Associate at Indian Institute of Technology Delhi, New Delhi, India

**Funded Research Projects:**

- Energy Efficient Lighting with VLC and PLC based Communications  funded by DST, GoI and  IIT Jammu (On Going)
- Improved PHY and MAC strategies for M2M Communications in Smart Grid over Wireless and PLC Heterogeneous Network funded by SERB, DST, GoI (Closed)
- Cooperative Isolated Renewable Energy Systems for Enhancing Reliability of Power in Rural Areas funded by DST, GoI and IIT Jammu (On Going)

##### Publications

**Journals:**

1. **A. Dubey**, R. K. Mallik, and R. Schober, “Performance analysis of a PLC system employing SC in correlated log-normal channels and impulsive noise," *IET Communications*, vol. 8, no. 7, pp. 1072-1082, May 2014.
2. **A. Dubey**, R. K. Mallik, and R. Schober, “Performance analysis of a multi-hop PLC system over log-normal fading in presence of impulsive noise,” *IET Communications*, vol. 9, no. 1, pp. 1-9, Jan. 2015.
3. **A. Dubey** and R. K. Mallik, “PLC system performance with AF relaying," *IEEE Transactions on Communications*, vol. 63, no. 6, pp. 2337-2345, June 2015.
4. **A. Dubey** and R. K. Mallik, “Effect of channel correlation and impulsive noise on multi-hop data transmission over power cables with DF relays," *IET Communications*, vol. 10, no. 13, pp. 1623-1630, Sep. 2016.
5. D. Sharma, **A. Dubey**, S. Mishra, and R. K. Mallik, “A frequency control strategy using power line communication in a smart microgrid,” *IEEE Access,*vol. 7, no., pp. 21712-21721, Feb. 2019.
6. **A. Dubey**, C. Kundu, T. M. N. Ngatched, O. A. Dobre, and R. K. Mallik, “Incremental relaying for power line communications: performance analysis and power allocation," *IEEE Systems Journal*, vol. 13, no. 4, pp. 4236-4247, Mar. 2019.
7. Y. S. Reddy, M. Panda, **A. Dubey**, A. Kumar, T. Panigrahi, and K. Rabie, “Optimization of indoor hybrid PLC/VLC/RF communication systems," *IET Communications*, vol. 14, no. 1, pp. 117-126, Oct. 2019.
8. A. M. Wilson, T. Panigrahi, and **A. Dubey**, “Robust distributed Lorentzian adaptive filter with diffusion strategy in impulsive noise environment," *Digital Signal Processing*, vol. 96, pp. 102589, Jan. 2020.
9. Y. S. Reddy, **A. Dubey**, A. Kumar, and T. Panigrahi, “A successive interference cancellation based random access channel mechanism for machine-to-machine communications in cellular Internet-of-Things," *IEEE Access*, vol. 9, pp. 8367-8380, Jan. 2021.
10. Y. S. Reddy, M. Panda, **A. Dubey**, A. Kumar, and T. Panigrahi, “A probabilistic approach to model SIC based RACH mechanism for machine type communications in cellular networks," *IEEE Transaction on Vehicular Technology*, accepted for publication in Jan. 2021.
11. P. K. Hota, S. Thapar, D. Mishra, R. Saini, and **A. Dubey,** “Ergodic performance of downlink untrusted NOMA system with imperfect SIC,” *IEEE Communications Letters*, accepted for publication in Nov. 2021.
12. A. Girdher, A. Bansal, and **A. Dubey**, “On the performance of SLIPT-enabled DF relay-aided hybrid OW/RF network," accepted for publication at IEEE Systems Journal, in Dec 2021.

**Conferences –**

1. **A. Dubey**, R. K. Mallik, and R. Schober, “Performance of a PLC system in impulsive noise with selection combining," in *Proc. the IEEE Global Communications Conference (GLOBECOM)*, Anaheim, USA, Dec. 3-7, 2012, pp. 3508 - 3512.
2. **A. Dubey**, D. Sharma, R. K. Mallik, and S. Mishra, “Modeling and performance analysis of a PLC system in presence of impulsive noise," in *Proc.* *the* *2015 IEEE Power & Energy Society General Meeting*, Denver, USA, July 26-30, 2015, pp.1-5.
3. D. Sharma, R. K. Mallik, S. Mishra, **A. Dubey**, and V. Ranjan, “Voltage control of a DC microgrid with double-input converter in a multi-PV scenario using PLC," in *Proc.* *the 2016 IEEE Power & Energy Society General Meeting*, Boston, USA, July 17-21, 2016, pp.1-5.
4. **A. Dubey**, C. Kundu, T. M. N. Ngatched, O. A. Dobre, and R. K. Mallik, “Performance of incremental decode-and-forward relaying in power-line communication," in *Proc. 2017 IEEE 86th Vehicular Technology Conference (VTC-Fall)*, Toronto, ON, 2017, pp. 1-6.
5. Y. S. Reddy, **A. Dubey**, and A. Kumar, "A novel RACH mechanism for machine type communications in cellular networks," *2017 IEEE International Conference on Advanced Networks and Telecommunications Systems (ANTS)*, Bhubaneswar, 2017, pp. 1-6

7. Y. S. Reddy, **A. Dubey**, and A. Kumar, "A MAC-PHY cross-layer analysis of NB-PLC system in presence of impulsive noise," *2018 10th International Conference on Communication Systems & Networks (COMSNETS)*, Bengaluru, 2018, pp. 384-387.
8. B. P. Mishra, T. Panigrahi and **A. Dubey**, "Robust distributed estimation of wireless channel," in *Proc. 2018 International Conference on Applied Electromagnetics, Signal Processing and Communication (AESPC)*, Bhubaneswar, India, 2018, pp. 1-5.
9. K. P. Sumesh, **A. Dubey**, and T. Panigrahi, "Hardware implementation of filtered OFDM for BB-PLC using software defined radio," in *Proc.* *2019 National Conference on Communications (NCC)*, Bangalore, India, 2019, pp. 1-6.
10. G. Chopra, Y. Ramamoorthi, A. Kumar, and **A. Dubey,**“Non-orthogonal multiple access for ultra-dense cellular networks with base station sleeping,” *in Proc. the 2020 IEEE 3rd 5G World Forum (5GWF),*held virtually.
11. B. Wafai, C. Kundu, **A. Dubey**, J. Jhang, and M. Flanagan, “Transmitter selection for secrecy in cognitive small-cell networks with backhaul knowledge,” accepted for presentation at 2021 *IEEE 93rd Vehicular Technology Conference (VTC-Spring)*, to be held at Helsinki, Finland, between 25-28 Apr. 2021.
12. S. Bhushan, C. Kundu, S Modem, **A. Dubey**, and M. Flanagan, “Transmitter selection for secrecy in frequency selective fading channel with unreliable backhaul,” accepted for presentation at 2021 *IEEE 93rd Vehicular Technology Conference (VTC-Spring)*, to be held at Helsinki, Finland, between 25-28 Apr. 2021.
13. A. Girdher, A. Bansal, and **A. Dubey**, “Analyzing SLIPT for DF based mixed FSO-RF communication system,” in *Proc. 28th International Conference on Telecommunications*, 1-3 June, London, UK, pp. 1-7.
14. Y. S. Reddy, G. Chopra, **A. Dubey**, A. Kumar, T. Panigrahi, and L.R. Cenkeramaddi, “Rate-splitting random access mechanism for massive machine type communications in 5G cellular internet-of-things,” in *Proc. IEEE International Symposium on Personal, Indoor and Mobile Radio Communications (PIMRC) 2021*, Virtual, 13–16 Sep. 2021, pp. 648-653.
15. A. Girdher, A. Bansal, and **A. Dubey**, “'Level crossing rate and average fade duration of RIS-assisted RF communication system," in *Proc. IEEE INDICON 2021*, 19-21 December, 2021, Guwahati, India, pp. 1-6.

Biography:

Ankit received the B.E. degree in Electronics and Telecommunication Engineering from the Chhattisgarh Swami Vivekanand Technical University (CSVTU), Bhilai-India in 2009 and the Ph.D. degree in Electrical Engineering from the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT), Delhi-India in 2014. In 2012 and 2013, he was a visiting research scholar at the University of British Columbia, Vancouver, Canada. From July 2014 to December 2014 he has been a research associate with IIT Delhi. From December 2014 to Dec 2018, he has been with the faculty of the Department of Electronics and Communication Engineering, National Institute of Technology (NIT), Goa-India, where he was an Assistant Professor. Since January 2019, he has been with the faculty of the Department of Electrical Engineering, Indian Institute of Technology (IIT), Jammu-India, where he is currently an Assistant Professor and Head of the Department. He has published several journal and conference papers in the area of communications engineering. He has several govt. of India sponsored projects worth 15 Millions INR.  He is also working on multidisciplinary research project on indigenous UAV systems funded by IIT Jammu with fund up to the tune of 40 Million INR. His research interests are in diversity combining, multi-hop transmission, and physical layer security, PLC, IoT, and wireless communications. He works in the application side for smart grid communications, automation, IoT, UAV detection using radar, etc.

(SERB), Government of India.

Government of India.

Technology, Government of India.

Electronics and Information Technology, Government of India.

Designs for Space Applications, Funding Agency: Science and Engineering Research
Board (SERB), Government of India.

self noise cancellation in underwater acoustics.

Electrical Engineering | IIT Jammu

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/logo_ee_preloader.png)

![Breadcrumbs Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/banner_all.png)

- [Home](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)
- Ankur Bansal

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in//facultyImages/Ankur Bansal_Image.jpg)

- Ankur Bansal
- Associate Professor
- ankur.bansal@iitjammu.ac.in

- [Brief Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ankurbansal#prod-overview)
- [Profile](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ankurbansal#prod-curriculum)
- [Current Openings](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ankurbansal#prod-currentopenings)
- [Other Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ankurbansal#prod-reviews)
- [Personal Website](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ankurbansal#prod-personalwebsite)

#### Ankur Bansal

##### Education Qualification

- M. TECH. (SIGNAL PROCESSING) 2007-2009 NSIT DELHI,
- PH. D. (WIRELESS COMMUNICATION) 2010-2013 IIT DELHI

##### Academic Interests

**Research Interests**

- Cooperative communications
- Multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) systems
- Distributed space-time block code (DSTBC) based communication systems
- Multiuser communications
- Free space optical (FSO) communication systems
- Mixed RF and FSO systems
- Power line communication (PLC) systems
- 5G Wireless Communications
- Non-orthogonal multiple access (NOMA).

**Teaching Interests**

Probability and Stochastic processes, Digital Communication, Signal Theory, Wireless Communications, Detection and Estimation Theory

##### Research Experience

**Teaching & Research:**

Sep. 2013- Dec. 2019 NSIT Delhi (Currently NSUT Delhi)

##### Publications

- Ankur Bansal, Manav R. Bhatnagar, and Are Hjørungnes, “Decoding and Performance Bound of Demodulate-and-Forward Based Distributed Alamouti STBC,” in IEEE Transactions on Wireless Communications, vol. 12, no. 2, pp. 702-713, Feb. 2013.
- Ankur Bansal, Manav R. Bhatnagar, Are Hjørungnes, and Zhu Han, “Low Complexity Decoding in DF MIMO Relaying System,” in IEEE Transactions on Vehicular Technology, vol. 62, no. 3, pp. 1123-1137, Mar. 2013.
- Prabhat Kumar Sharma, Ankur Bansal, and Parul Garg, “Relay Assisted Bi-directional Communication in Generalized Turbulence Fading,” in IEEE Journal of Lightwave Technology, vol. 33, no. 1, pp 133-139, Jan. 2015.
- Neha Singhal, Ankur Bansal and Ashwni Kumar, “Performance Evaluation of DF Based Asymmetric SIMO-RF/FSO System with Misalignment Errors”, IET Communications, Vol. 11, Issue 14, pp 2244-2252, July 2017.
- Deepti Agarwal and Ankur Bansal, “Unified Error Performance of Multihop DF-FSO Network with Aperture Averaging”, in IEEE/OSA Journal of Optical Communications and Networking, Vol. 11, Issue. 3, pp 95-106, January 2019.

Vision and Mission

## Powering the Generations

To ensure excellence across a wide range of disciplines, professions, and arts while
also encouraging investigation across disciplinary boundaries with creative learning.

To nurture holistic engineers and to address global challenges through research,
innovation, inspiration, and influence.

[Read
More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/department-vision-mission.html)

2023.

### [VDAT 2022](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

VDAT began as a small workshop in the year 1998. In 2005, it acquired
the status of a Symposium. The purpose of the Symposium is to promote the
advancement of all aspects of VLSI.

23rd June 2022.

Laboratories

## Undergraduate and Postgraduate Labs

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/Underwater.jpg)

#### Underwater Research Lab

#### [Underwater Research lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

At IIT Jammu a unique and first kind of research platform is developed
with a size of 25ft x 20ft which is having similar facility of ocean including the
waves and artificial noise injection process in ocean.

[Read More](https://www.iitjammu.ac.in/underwater-artificial-intelligence-lab)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/aadhrit.JPG)

#### AADHRIT Lab

#### [AADHRIT Lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

AADHRIT Lab is designed to test and demonstrate the real-time operation
of Micro/Smart Grid solutions developed by the research group.

[Read More](https://www.aadhritlab.org/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/low voltage lab 1.JPG)

#### Low Voltage Lab1

#### [Low Voltage Lab1](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

This lab is furnished with thirty numbers of high configuration
desktops.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/low v lab 2.JPG)

#### Low Voltage Lab 2

#### [Low Voltage Lab 2](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

This lab lays the foundation stone for students of Electrical
Engineering.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/high voltage lab.JPG)

#### High Voltage Lab

#### [High Voltage Lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

Equipped with various high voltage equipments like transformers, motors,
generators, winding machines, the place gives experience of hands-on learning.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/anechoic chamber.JPG)

#### Anechoic Chamber

#### [Anechoic Chamber](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

This lab established in 2018, is a specialized facility established for
interference free measurements of various parameters of antennas and other microwave
devices.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/IC reliability, security lab.JPG)

#### IC Reliabality, Security & Quality Laboratory

#### [IC Reliabality, Security & Quality Laboratory](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

Research is being carried out to meet the challenges in Very Large Scale
Integration based design of circuits.

[Read More](https://www.iitjammu.ac.in/aadhrit-lab/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/prototype design and development lab.JPG)

#### Prototype Design and Development Lab

#### [Prototype Design and Development Lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/)

This is a dedicated lab for research especially in the field of
Robotics, Iot and embedded systems.

[Read More](https://www.iitjammu.ac.in/aadhrit-lab/)

## From The Desk of HoD

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/Ravikant Saini.jpg)

Welcome to the Department of Electrical Engineering, Indian Institute of
Technology Jammu. In line with the Institute's focus on
academics-oriented research, the department considers both teaching and
research integral. The department accommodates highly experienced and
dedicated faculty members who are great teachers and researchers in
their respective domains. We are also supported by invaluable staff
members who discharge their duties efficiently and enthusiastically on
the technical and administrative front. We look for zealous young minds
for our UG, PG, and PhD programs, as they are our greatest strength.

Dr. Ravikant Saini
Head of Department

[Read
More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/hod.html)

Institute of Technology (IIT) Jammu, has been awarded a generous grant

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/awards/farah-nazrreceives-serb-international-travel-support.jpeg)

### [IEEE NEWCAS 2023: Ms Farah Naz receives SERB International

# Startups

- [Home](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)
- Startups

![About Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/startup/startup_1.jpg)

Startups at Department of Electrical Engineering, IIT Jammu

Dr. Ankit Dubey has mentored a startup named as Data Sailors.
The startup was initially a B.Tech. project by Mr. Kuldeep and Mr. Ayush (2020 Batch of
IIT Jammu). Data Sailors is mainly focused on resource monitoring, data analytics, and
forecasting using AI ML. Currently, the Data Sailors is incubated at IIT Jammu.

![About Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/startup/startup_2.jpg)

Dr. Sudhakar Modem has collaboration with Servotech private
limited and actively working on commercialization of products. First commercialized
product of oxygen concentrated already serving in India and foreign countries with >1500
units. Second product is on pilot phase implementation which is designed for GIZ
Germany- MNRE India-Servotech Ltd. project.

Electrical Engineering | IIT Jammu

- Ibhanchand Rath

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in//faculty/documents/images/1770706900894.jpeg)

- Ibhanchand Rath
- Assistant Professor
- ibhanchand.rath@iitjammu.ac.in

- [Brief Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ibhanchandrath#prod-overview)
- [Profile](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ibhanchandrath#prod-curriculum)
- [Current Openings](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ibhanchandrath#prod-currentopenings)
- [Other Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ibhanchandrath#prod-reviews)
- [Personal Website](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ibhanchandrath#prod-personalwebsite)

#### Ibhanchand Rath

Ibhan Chand Rath received the B.Tech. degree in Electrical and Electronics Engineering from the International Institute of Information Technology, Bhubaneswar, India, in 2014, and the Ph.D. degree in Electrical Engineering from IIT Bombay, India, in 2024. He worked as a System Integration and Testing Consultant at Igrenenergi Services Private Limited, Research Park, IIT BOMBAY, from May 2024 to December 2025. Currently, he is serving as Assistant Professor in the Electrical Engineering Department of IIT JAMMU from January 2026.

##### Research Interest

Grid connected hybrid multivelvel converter topology design, Flexible AC Transmission Systems (FACTs), High Voltage Direct Current (HVDC), Grid integration of Battery Energy Storage Systems (BESS), Battery Management System (BMS), V2G and G2V EV charging applications,

##### Education Qualification

Bachelor of Technology (B.Tech)

International Institute of Information Technology (IIIT), Bhubaneswar

Department: Electrical & Electronics Engineering

Duration: 2010 – 2014

Ph.D. (Direct PhD after B.Tech)

Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Bombay

Department: Electrical Engineering

Scheme: Visvesvaraya PhD Scheme for Electronics & IT

Duration: December 2015 – August 2024

##### Academic Interests

Power Electronics, power systems, electric machines, and control systems

##### Research Experience

**Doctoral Research Experience**

Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Bombay

Duration: 2015 – 2024

Areas of Research:

i. Development of hybrid multilevel power converter topologies for FACTS and HVDC applications.

ii. Power quality improvement of three phase AC grids, including reactive power compensation, unbalance mitigation, and harmonic compensation.

iii. Control algorithm development for capacitor voltage regulation in multilevel converters under unbalanced three-phase conditions.

iv. Application of multilevel converters for simultaneous charging of multiple electric vehicles (EVs).

**Industry Research Experience**

IgrenEnergi Services Private Limited

Duration: 2024 – 2025

Area of Work: Development of Battery Management Systems (BMS) for two- and four-wheeler electric vehicles, including passive and active cell balancing of battery packs

##### Publications

1. I. C. Rath, R. Shahane and A. Shukla, "A Split Phase Transformer-less Hybrid Converter STATCOM and its Capacitor Voltage Balancing," in IEEE Transactions on Power Electronics, doi: 10.1109/TPEL.2025.3639488
2. I. C. Rath, S. K. Patro and A. Shukla, "Transformer-Less Hybrid Series Static Compensator and its DC Capacitor Voltage Balance Technique Using Zero-Sequence Voltage," in IEEE Transactions on Power Electronics, vol. 39, no. 3, pp. 3244-3262, March 2024, doi: 10.1109/TPEL.2023.3336195.
3. I. C. Rath, S. K. Patro and A. Shukla, "Parallel-Hybrid Converter Based STATCOM: Operating Principles and Capacitor Voltage Control Using Fundamental Frequency Zero-Sequence Voltage," in IEEE Transactions on Power Electronics, vol. 37, no. 10, pp. 12134-12150, Oct. 2022, doi: 10.1109/TPEL.2022.3175321.
4. I. C. Rath, S. K. Patro and A. Shukla, "Parallel Hybrid Converter-Based STATCOM and Capacitor Voltage Control Technique," in IEEE Journal of Emerging and Selected Topics in Power Electronics, vol. 9, no. 5, pp. 5597-5612, Oct. 2021, doi: 10.1109/JESTPE.2021.3049867.
5. M. S. Ansari, I. C. Rath, S. K. Patro, A. Shukla and H. J. Bahirat, "High Power Parallel Hybrid DC-DC Converter," in IEEE Transactions on Industry Applications, vol. 59, no. 1, pp. 1077-1089, Jan.-Feb. 2023, doi: 10.1109/TIA.2022.3217026.

Electrical Engineering | IIT Jammu

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/logo_ee_preloader.png)

![Breadcrumbs Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/banner_all.png)

- [Home](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)
- Ambika Prasad Shah

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in//facultyImages/Ambika_image.jpg)

- Ambika Prasad Shah
- Associate Professor
- ambika.shah@iitjammu.ac.in

- [Brief Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ambikaprasadshah#prod-overview)
- [Profile](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ambikaprasadshah#prod-curriculum)
- [Current Openings](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ambikaprasadshah#prod-currentopenings)
- [Other Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ambikaprasadshah#prod-reviews)
- [Personal Website](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~ambikaprasadshah#prod-personalwebsite)

#### Ambika Prasad Shah

Dr. Ambika Prasad Shah is currently working as an Associate Professor in Electrical Engineering Department at the Indian Institute of Technology Jammu, India. He received Ph.D. degree from the Electrical Engineering Department, Indian Institute of Technology Indore, India. Before joining IIT Jammu, Dr. Shah worked as a Postdoctoral Fellow at the Institute for Microelectronics, TU Vienna, Austria.

He is the recipient of the Young Scientist Award from the M.P. Council of Science and Technology Bhopal, M.P. India. He received a Young Faculty Research Fellowship (YFRF) from the Ministry of Electronics and Information Technology (MeitY), Government of India in 2025. He was nominated for the 10th BRICS Young Scientist Forum 2025 in Brazil by DST, Govt. of India. He is the recipient of the Best Paper Award for two consecutive years at the VDAT-2024 and VDAT-2025, Second Best Award at the 7th International Conference on Microelectronics, Circuits and Systems (Micro-2020), and was nominated for the Best Paper from 31st IEEE Conference on Very Large Scale Integration (VLSI-SoC 2023).

He has authored/co-authored more than 110 research papers in peer-reviewed international journals and conferences and authored two books. He was the Conference Organizing Chair for VDAT-2022, Fellowship Chair for VLSID-2022, Publicity Chair for iSES 2023, and Fellowship Chair for VDAT 2025. He coordinates the VLSI Society of India, Himalayan Region Chapter. He is the associate editor of IEEE Transactions on VLSI Systems and IEEE Transactions on Dependable and Secure Computing, editor of Nature Scientific Reports and IETE Journal of Research, and guest editor of Springer and Elsevier journals. He is a fellow of IETE, a senior member of IEEE, and a member of ACM, ISTE, and IEI.

His current research interest includes reliability analysis of digital circuits, circuits and systems for biomedical applications, fault-tolerant circuits, low-power high-performance circuit designs, and Hardware security primitives.

##### Research Interest

Reliability analysis of digital circuits, circuits and systems for biomedical applications, low-power high-performance circuit designs, In-memory computing, SRAM, and Hardware security primitives.

##### Education Qualification

- PhD from Indian Institute of Technology Indore in March 2020.

##### Academic Interests

- CMOS Digital Integrated Circuit Designs
- Low-power Circuits and Systems
- Analog Integrated Circuit Designs
- Semiconductor Memory Technologies
- Hardware Security

##### Research Experience

- Associate Professor in the Electrical Engineering Department, Indian Institute of Technology Jammu, India, from February 2026 to till date.
- Assistant Professor in the Electrical Engineering Department, Indian Institute of Technology Jammu, India, from March 2020 to February 2026.
- Post-doctoral Fellow at the Institute for Microelectronics, Technische Universität Wien (TU Wien), Vienna, Austria, from January 2019 to March 2020.
- JRF/SRF at Indian Institute of Technology Indore, India, from July 2016 to December 2018.
- Assistant Professor at the Institute of Engineering and Technology, DAVV Indore, India, from Aug. 2010 to July 2016.

##### Publications

**Please refer to:** https://scholar.google.com/citations?user=I2FeAtQAAAAJ&hl=en

##### Editorial Services

- Associate Editor, IEEE Transactions on Very Large Scale Integration (VLSI) Systems
- Associate Editor, IEEE Transactions on Dependable and Secure Computing
- Editor, IETE Journal of Research
- Editor, Nature Scientific Reports

##### Awards & honours

- Young Faculty Research Fellowship (YFRF) from the Ministry of Electronics and Information Technology (MeitY), January 2025.
- BRICS Young Scientist Fellow, September 2025.
- Young Scientist Award from M.P. Council of Science & Technology Bhopal, March 2018.
- Best Paper Award at the 28th International Symposium on VLSI Design and Test (VDAT 2024) in 2024.
- Best Paper Award at the 29th International Symposium on VLSI Design and Test (VDAT 2025) in 2025.
- Second Best Award at the 7th International Conference on Microelectronics, Circuits, and Systems (Micro-2020).

- [Personal Website](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~shikhabaghel#prod-personalwebsite)

#### Shikha Baghel

I am currently serving as an Assistant Professor in the Department of Electrical Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Jammu (IIT Jammu). Prior to this, I held faculty positions as an Assistant Professor in the Department of Electrical Engineering at IIT Tirupati and in the Department of Electronics and Communication Engineering at the National Institute of Technology Karnataka (NITK), Surathkal. Before transitioning to academia, I worked as a Postdoctoral Researcher in the LEAP Lab at the Indian Institute of Science (IISc) Bangalore. I earned my Ph.D. in Signal Processing from the Department of Electronics and Electrical Engineering at the Indian Institute of Technology Guwahati (IIT Guwahati). My research interests lie in the areas of speech and audio processing, speaker and language diarization, dialect and language identification, as well as the application of signal processing, machine learning, and deep learning techniques.

##### Research Interest

Speech and Audio Processing, Speaker Diarization, Language Diarization, Dialect/Language Identification, Applications of signal processing, Applications of Machine Learning and Deep Learning.

##### Education Qualification

1. Ph.D., IIT Guwahati, 2022
2. M.Tech., IIIT Allahabad, 2015
3. B.Tech., Uttar Pradesh Technical University, 2012

##### Academic Interests

Teaching Interests

1. Signals and Systems
2. Digital Signal Processing
3. Linear Algebra
4. Foundations of Machine Learning

##### Research Experience

1. Assistant Professor at EE Dept., Indian Institute of Technology Tirupati (IIT Tirupati), Dec. 2024-Jul.2025
2. Assistant Professor at ECE Dept., National Institute of Technology Karnataka (NITK), Surathkal, Dec. 2023-Nov. 2024
3. PostDoc Researcher at LEAP Lab, Indian Institute of Science (IISc) Bangalore, Aug. 2022-Nov. 2023

##### Publications

1. S. Baghel, S. Ramoji, S. Jain, P. R. Chowdhuri, P. Singh, D. Vijayasenan, and S. Ganapathy, “Summary of the DISPLACE challenge 2023-DIarization of SPeaker and LAnguage in Conversational Environments", Speech Communication, vol. 161, pp. 103080:1-15, 2024.
2. S. Baghel, S. Ramoji, Sidharth, Ranjana H, P. Singh, S. Jain, P. Roy Chowdhuri, K. Kulkarni, S. Padhi, D. Vijayasenan, S. Ganapathy, “DISPLACE Challenge: DIarization of SPeaker and LAnguage in Conversational Environments", INTERSPEECH, Aug. 2023, pp. 3562–3566.
3. M. Tzudir, S. Baghel, P. Sarmah, and S. R. M. Prasanna, “Exploration of an Under-Resourced Dialect Identification in Ao using Source Information", The Journal of the Acoustical Society of America (JASA), vol. 152, no. 3, pp. 1755–1766, 2022.
4. S. Baghel, S. R. M. Prasanna, and P. Guha, “Overlapped speech detection using phase features", The Journal of the Acoustical Society of America (JASA), vol. 150, no. 4, pp. 2770-2781, 2021.
5. S. Baghel, S. R. M. Prasanna, and P. Guha, “Exploration of Excitation Source Information for Shouted and Normal Speech Classification", The Journal of the Acoustical Society of America (JASA), vol. 147, no. 2, pp. 1250-1261, 2020.

Vision and Mission

## Powering the Generations

To ensure excellence across a wide range of disciplines, professions, and arts while
also encouraging investigation across disciplinary boundaries with creative learning.

To nurture holistic engineers and to address global challenges through research,
innovation, inspiration, and influence.

Laboratories

## Undergraduate and Postgraduate Labs

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/Underwater.jpg)

#### Underwater Research Lab

#### [Underwater Research lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

At IIT Jammu a unique and first kind of research platform is developed
with a size of 25ft x 20ft which is having similar facility of ocean including the
waves and artificial noise injection process in ocean.

[Read More](https://www.iitjammu.ac.in/underwater-artificial-intelligence-lab)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/aadhrit.JPG)

#### AADHRIT Lab

#### [AADHRIT Lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

AADHRIT Lab is designed to test and demonstrate the real-time operation
of Micro/Smart Grid solutions developed by the research group.

[Read More](https://www.aadhritlab.org/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/low voltage lab 1.JPG)

#### Low Voltage Lab1

#### [Low Voltage Lab1](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

This lab is furnished with thirty numbers of high configuration
desktops.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/low v lab 2.JPG)

#### Low Voltage Lab 2

#### [Low Voltage Lab 2](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

This lab lays the foundation stone for students of Electrical
Engineering.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/high voltage lab.JPG)

#### High Voltage Lab

#### [High Voltage Lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

Equipped with various high voltage equipments like transformers, motors,
generators, winding machines, the place gives experience of hands-on learning.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/anechoic chamber.JPG)

#### Anechoic Chamber

#### [Anechoic Chamber](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

This lab established in 2018, is a specialized facility established for
interference free measurements of various parameters of antennas and other microwave
devices.

[Read More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/IC reliability, security lab.JPG)

#### IC Reliabality, Security & Quality Laboratory

#### [IC Reliabality, Security & Quality Laboratory](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

Research is being carried out to meet the challenges in Very Large Scale
Integration based design of circuits.

[Read More](https://www.iitjammu.ac.in/aadhrit-lab/)

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/labs/prototype design and development lab.JPG)

#### Prototype Design and Development Lab

#### [Prototype Design and Development Lab](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)

This is a dedicated lab for research especially in the field of
Robotics, Iot and embedded systems.

[Read More](https://www.iitjammu.ac.in/aadhrit-lab/)

## From The Desk of HoD

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/assets/images/electrical/Ravikant Saini.jpg)

Welcome to the Department of Electrical Engineering, Indian Institute of
Technology Jammu. In line with the Institute's focus on
academics-oriented research, the department considers both teaching and
research integral. The department accommodates highly experienced and
dedicated faculty members who are great teachers and researchers in
their respective domains. We are also supported by invaluable staff
members who discharge their duties efficiently and enthusiastically on
the technical and administrative front. We look for zealous young minds
for our UG, PG, and PhD programs, as they are our greatest strength.

Dr. Ravikant Saini
Head of Department

[Read
More](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/hod.html)

- [Home](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/index.html)
- Kushmanda Saurav

![Image](https://iitjammu.ac.in//faculty/documents/images/1642482807324.jpeg)

- Kushmanda Saurav
- Associate Professor
- saurav.kushmanda@iitjammu.ac.in

- [Brief Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~kushmandasaurav#prod-overview)
- [Profile](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~kushmandasaurav#prod-curriculum)
- [Current Openings](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~kushmandasaurav#prod-currentopenings)
- [Other Info](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~kushmandasaurav#prod-reviews)
- [Personal Website](https://iitjammu.ac.in/ee/faculty.html?faculty=~kushmandasaurav#prod-personalwebsite)

#### Kushmanda Saurav

##### Education Qualification

Ph.D.   Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur, India, 2017

M. Tech.  Indian Institute of Technology Roorkee, 2011

B. E.    Bengal Engineering and Science University, Shibpur, 2009

##### Academic Interests

**COURSES TAUGHT AT IIT JAMMU**

- **ELL 212 Engineering Electromagnetics**
- **ELP 212 Engineering Electromagnetics Lab**
- **ELL 202 Circuit Theory**
- **ELL 304 Analog Electronics**
- **EFL005U1M Basic Electronics Engineering**
- **EFP005U1M Basic Electronics Engineering Lab**
- **EEL006P1M Antenna and Wave Propagation**
- **EEL003P1M R.F. System**
- **EEP003P1M R.F. System Lab**
- **EEP016U3M Analog Electronics Lab**

##### Research Experience

- **Post-Doctoral Fellow in the Department of Electrical Engineering at Royal Military College Canada from November 2016 to October 2017.**
- **Assistant Professor in the Department of Electrical Engineering at Indian Institute of Technology Jammu from October 2017 to till date.**

##### Publications

**LIST OF PUBLICATIONS**

**Journal Papers:**

1. Mehran Manzoor Zargar, Archana Rajput, **Kushmand Saurav** and S. K. Koul, "Low RCS Dual-Polarized Crossed Dipole Antenna Co-Designed with Absorptive Frequency-Selective Reflection Structure," accepted for publication in ***IEEE Access***, vol. 10, pp. 118806-118814, 2022, DOI: 10.1109/ACCESS.2022.3220672. Impact Factor: 3.476.
2. Mohammad Ayoub Sofi, **Kushmanda Saurav**, S K Koul, "Linear-to-Circular Polarization Converter with Wide Angular Stability and Near Unity Ellipticity-Application to Linearly Polarized Antenna Array," in ***IEEE Transactions on Circuits and Systems II: Express Briefs***, vol. 69, no. 12, pp. 4779-4783, Dec. 2022, DOI: 10.1109/TCSII.2022.3196385. Impact Factor: 3.691
3. Mehran Manzoor Zargar, Archana Rajput, **Kushmand Saurav** and S. K. Koul, "Frequency-Selective Rasorber Based on High-Q Minkowski Fractal-Shaped Resonator for Realizing a Low Radar Cross-Section Radiating System," in ***IEEE Transactions on Electromagnetic Compatibility***, vol. 64, no. 5, pp. 1574-1584, Oct. 2022, DOI: 10.1109/TEMC.2022.3179514. Impact Factor: 2.036. Citation 02.

#### Satyadev Ahlawat

##### Education Qualification

- Ph.D. in Electrical Engineering (2014 - 2018): Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Bombay, India
- M.Tech. in Microelectronics (2008 - 2010): Panjab University (PU), Chandigarh, India
- M.Sc. in Electronic Science (2006 - 2008): Kurukshetra University (KU), Kurukshetra, India
- B.Sc. in Electronics (2002 - 2005): Maharshi Dayanand University (MDU), Rohtak, India

##### Academic Interests

Research Interests:

VLSI Testing and Design-for-Testability (DfT), Trusted System Design, Hardware Security, High Performance Processor Design

Teaching Interests:

VLSI Design and Test, Cryptography and Hardware Security, Semiconductor Device Physics and Technology, Computer Architecture

##### Research Experience

- Assistant Professor (July 2019 - Present): Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Jammu, India
- Research Scientist (Sep. 2018 - July 2019): Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Bombay, India
- Teaching Assistant (July 2014 - Aug. 2018): Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Bombay, India
- Lecturer (Sep. 2012 - June 2013): Kurukshetra University (KU), Kurukshetra, India
- Research Associate (Dec. 2011 - Aug. 2012): Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) Bombay, India
- Research Assistant (Aug. 2010 - Nov. 2011): Indian Institute of Science (IISc) Bangalore, India

#### Arun Kumar Verma

Dr. Verma earned his master’s and Ph.D. from I.I.T. Delhi, New Delhi, India. He served as a visiting professor at Ontario Tech University, Oshawa, Ontario, Canada, in 2024. He was a Postdoctoral research fellow (PDF) at the Energy Research Institute (ERI@N), Nanyang Technological University (NTU) Singapore, from 2015 to 2016. Before joining NTU Singapore, he worked as a visiting graduate researcher (VGR) at the Smart Grid Energy Research Center (SMERC), University of California, Los Angeles (UCLA), California, USA, from 2014 to 2015. He won the prestigious BASE fellowship for advanced solar energy research in 2014. He has been conferred with the prestigious POSOCO Power System Research Award 2016. He was also selected for the SERB International Research Experience (SIRE) award in 2023. He is an associate Editor for IEEE Transactions on Transportation Electrification and an associate editor for IEEE Journal of Emerging and Selected Topics in Industrial Electronics, as well as an assistant editor of the Smart Grid journal and a member of the editorial board for the EPE Journal. He has been invited by Defence University College, Ethiopia, and Metal Engineering Corporation, Ethiopia, as an instructor for the M.Tech program in Renewable Energy Engineering from 7 May 2016 to 27 May 2016. To name a few. He has/completed DST research funding of 7.5 cr., including Mission Innovation (MI), SPARC, ECR, SERD, and CRG. He is also the mentor director of a startup, Rishi Agastaya Technologies Pvt. Ltd. Dr Verma has guided 10 PhD and 18 M.Tech theses. Six PhD candidates are currently working under his supervision.

##### Research Interest

Power electronics, converters for renewable energy and EV chargers, bi-directional power flow, and electric transportation. Sustainable and intelligent Off-Grid solar PV system, On-board EV chargers, and  Fast EV chargers

##### Education Qualification

- **Ph.D. Electrical Engineering**  Indian Institute of Technology (I.I.T.) Delhi, New Delhi-1110016.
- Thesis Title: Analysis, design and control of solar photovoltaic energy integration for smart grid distribution systems.
- **Master of Technology (MTech), in Energy Studies**  Indian Institute of Technology (I.I.T.) Delhi, New Delhi, .
- Thesis Title: Design, Modeling and Control of Isolated Solar Photovoltaic Power Generation Systems.
- **Bachelor of Engineering (B.E), Electrical Engineering**, DCRUST Murthal Formerly C.R State College of Engineering Murthal, Sonepat, Harayana,

##### Academic Interests

**Research Areas**

Power Electronics, Converters for Electric Vehicle Chargers and Renewable Energy, Renewable Integration Grid, Smart Grid and Smart Buildings, Electric Vehicle (EV) Integration to Grid, Bi-directional Power Flow.

**Research Interests**

Electric Vehicles infrastructure, DC-DC/DC-AC Converters for EV and renewable energy

#### Anup Shukla

Dr. Anup Shukla (Senior Member IEEE, Power and Energy Society, Industry Applications Society, IEEE Young Professionals). From June 2016 to Dec 2016, He was with the Department of Electrical Engineering, Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur as Senior Project Engineer. From Jan 2017 to Aug. 2017, He was with the Department of Electrical Engineering and Computer Science Engineering, Howard University, USA as Post-Doctorate. He is currently working as Visiting Faculty at Loughborough University from October 2023 to April 2024. He is currently working as an Associate Professor with the Department of Electrical Engineering, Indian Institute of Technology Jammu, India. He was the recipient of POSOCO Power System Award, 2017 and Dr. P.S. Nigam Power Sector Award, 2013.

##### Research Interest

His current research interest includes Robust and efficient system operation and planning, Renewable integration in power systems, Power system security, Power System Restructuring /Deregulation, Distribution System and Micro/Smart Grid

##### Education Qualification

**Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur, India***July 2011-May 2016*

**Ph.D** in Electrical Engineering

***Supervisor***: Prof. S.N.Singh

***Thesis***: Evolutionary Techniques Based Solution to the Unit Commitment Problem Including Renewable Energy Sources.

**PEC University of Technology Chandigarh, India***July 2007-July 2009*

**M.E in Power System**

##### Academic Interests

- Robust and efficient system operation and planning.
- Uncertainty modelling.
- Renewable integration in power systems.
- Power system security.
- Power System Restructuring /Deregulation.
- Distributed Generations and Smart Grid.

##### Research Experience

**A Multi-Dimentional Smart Energy Grids Analysis for Indian Scenario**

Indian Institute of Technology Kanpur, India Jun. 2016- Nov. 2016 Sponsoring Agency: Department of Science and Technology

With: Prof. S.N.Singh

- Involved in the development of a shared and cross-disciplinary understanding of smart grid systems and distributed storage facilities for urban and rural areas in India.
- Implementation of Optimization techniques to solve the problem of smart energy grid with the integration renewable energy resources.

**Engineering Design and Implementation of Aerial Protection Scheme for Lightning Strike on ICC Box**

Howard University, Washington DC Jan. 2017- August 2017 Sponsoring Agency: Federal Aviation Administration

With: Prof. James Momoh

- Development & Implementation of design of micro-based control of protecting the ICC box directly. This is referred to as design of Advanced Transient Protection box called the Howard University box.
- Develop Technical Instruction Book (TIB) for the Howard University Transient Protection box of 2000V/400V.

#### Kankat Ghosh

##### Research Interest

- Molecular Beam Epitaxy growth
- III-Nitride based Photodetector and LED
- Rare earth Oxides
- HEMT, MOSCAP
- Spectroscopy

##### Education Qualification

- 2018 Ph.D. in Electrical Engineering, Indian Institute of Technology Bombay, India,
- 2011 M.Tech. in Radio Physics and Electronics, University of Calcutta, India
- 2009 B.Tech. in Radio Physics and Electronics, University of Calcutta, India
- 2006 B.Sc. in Physics, University of Calcutta, India

##### Professional Background

- July '19 - Present: Assistant Professor at Indian Institute of Technology Jammu, Jammu, J&K, India
